    function generateRandomUuid() {
        var str =
            (navigator.userAgent || '') +
            (navigator.platform || '') +
            document.cookie +
            (new Date()).getTime() +
            Math.random()
        ;

        var
            rotate_left = function (n, s) {
                return (n << s) | (n >>> (32 - s));
            },

            cvt_hex = function (val) {
                var strout = '',
                    i,
                    v;

                for (i = 7; i >= 0; i--) {
                    v = (val >>> (i * 4)) & 0x0f;
                    strout += v.toString(16);
                }

                return strout;
            },

            blockstart,
            i,
            j,
            W = [],
            H0 = 0x67452301,
            H1 = 0xEFCDAB89,
            H2 = 0x98BADCFE,

            temp,
            str_len,
            word_array = [];

        for (i = 0; i < str_len - 3; i += 4) {
            j = str.charCodeAt(i) << 24 | str.charCodeAt(i + 1) << 16 |
                str.charCodeAt(i + 2) << 8 | str.charCodeAt(i + 3);
            word_array.push(j);
        }

        switch (str_len & 3) {
            case 0:
                i = 0x080000000;
                break;
            case 1:
                i = str.charCodeAt(str_len - 1) << 24 | 0x0800000;
                break;
            case 2:
                i = str.charCodeAt(str_len - 2) << 24 | str.charCodeAt(str_len - 1) << 16 | 0x08000;
                break;
            case 3:
                i = str.charCodeAt(str_len - 3) << 24 | str.charCodeAt(str_len - 2) << 16 | str.charCodeAt(str_len - 1) << 8 | 0x80;
                break;
        }

        word_array.push(i);

        while ((word_array.length & 15) !== 14) {
            word_array.push(0);
        }

        word_array.push(str_len >>> 29);
        word_array.push((str_len << 3) & 0x0ffffffff);

        for (blockstart = 0; blockstart < word_array.length; blockstart += 16) {
            for (i = 0; i < 16; i++) {
                W[i] = word_array[blockstart + i];
            }

            }

            for (i = 20; i <= 39; i++) {
                temp = (rotate_left(A, 5) + (B ^ C ^ D) + E + W[i] + 0x6ED9EBA1) & 0x0ffffffff;
                E = D;
                D = C;
                C = rotate_left(B, 30);
                B = A;
                A = temp;
            }

            for (i = 40; i <= 59; i++) {
                temp = (rotate_left(A, 5) + ((B & C) | (B & D) | (C & D)) + E + W[i] + 0x8F1BBCDC) & 0x0ffffffff;
                E = D;
                D = C;
                C = rotate_left(B, 30);
                B = A;
                A = temp;
            }

            for (i = 60; i <= 79; i++) {
                temp = (rotate_left(A, 5) + (B ^ C ^ D) + E + W[i] + 0xCA62C1D6) & 0x0ffffffff;
                E = D;
                D = C;
                C = rotate_left(B, 30);
                B = A;
                A = temp;
            }

            H0 = (H0 + A) & 0x0ffffffff;
            H1 = (H1 + B) & 0x0ffffffff;
            H2 = (H2 + C) & 0x0ffffffff;
            H3 = (H3 + D) & 0x0ffffffff;
            H4 = (H4 + E) & 0x0ffffffff;
        }

        temp = cvt_hex(H0) + cvt_hex(H1) + cvt_hex(H2) + cvt_hex(H3) + cvt_hex(H4);

        return temp.toLowerCase().slice(0, 32);
    }

    function getCookie(NameOfCookie) {
        if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
            let begin = document.cookie.indexOf(NameOfCookie + '=')
            if (begin != -1) {
                begin += NameOfCookie.length + 1
                let end = document.cookie.indexOf(';', begin)
                if (end == -1) end = document.cookie.length
                return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end))
            }
        }
        return ''
    }

    dataLayer[0].email = getCookie('email');
    dataLayer[0].emailMd5 = getCookie('emailMd5');
    dataLayer[0].emailSha256 = getCookie('emailSha256');
    dataLayer[0].UserId = getCookie('userId');
    dataLayer[0].userType = dataLayer[0].UserId ? 'Member' : '';
    dataLayer[0].sessionCode = generateRandomUuid();
</script>

                                        <div class="faqs-question">
                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">1. How do I place an order?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>To place your order, simply follow the steps as shown below:
  <br />
 1. Go to the item page.
<br />
 2. Choose your preferred color and size (if applicable). 
  <br />
 3. Click "Add to Cart"
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-1-1.png" />
 <br />
 4. Review that everything is correct and click "Checkout".
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-1-2.png" />
 <br />
 5. Go to the checkout page.
 <br />
 6. If you're a registered customer, sign in first. If you're a new customer, checkout as guest now. 
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-1-3.png" />
 <br />
 7. Fill out all shipping and payment information. 
<br />
 8. Click "Place Order"
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-1-4.png" />
<br />
 You'll be taken to a confirmation page that will give you an order number and you will be emailed a confirmation once the payment has processed. Please be sure to read all emails from us carefully. 
<br />
 If you need further guidance or run into any issues when placing your order, please Contact Us, and we'll get back to you as soon as possible."</p>
                            <div class="hide-answer-box"><a class="faqs-article-link" target="_blank" href="https://jjshouse.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360039198034-How-to-place-an-order-?domain=www.jjshouse.com">Read Article<span></span></a></div>

                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">2. I ordered a standard-size dress, not a custom-made one. Why is it taking so long?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>All of our dresses are made to order, whether you ordered a standard or custom size, both require tailoring time. Tailoring Time is displayed on each dress's product page. 
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-2-1.png" />
 <br />
 If you've already placed an order, your estimated delivery date is in your Order Confirmation email. Or you can find it on the Order Details page via <a href="/account/order_status.php" target="_blank" style="font-weight: bold;">this link</a>. 
 <br / >
 Once your order has been shipped, we will email you a confirmation and tracking number with updated delivery information. Alternatively, you can retrieve the tracking number on the order details page via <a href="/account/order_status.php" target="_blank" style="font-weight: bold;">this link</a>. 
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-2-2.png" />
 <br />
 If your estimated delivery date has passed and you order hasn't been delivered, please Contact Us for further help.</p>

                                        <div class="faqs-question">
                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">4. When will I receive my order?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>Once you place an order, it will take us some time to either process or make the requested items before the order ships out to you. 
 <br />
 Estimated Receiving Time = Processing Time + Shipping Time
 <br />
 Before placing an order, you can check the specific processing time on Each Product page. The shipping time depends on shipping methods. The fastest shipping - expedited shipping takes 3-6 days for the shipment. The standard shipping takes 5-8 days. The super save shipping (only for orders of accessories valued less than $50) takes 15-30 days for the shipment. The sooner you place an order, the sooner we start preparing your item(s).
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-4-1.png" />
 <br />
 If you've already placed an order, your estimated delivery date is in your Order Confirmation email. Or you can find it on the Order Details page via this link. 
 <br />
 Once your order has been shipped, we will email you a confirmation and tracking number with updated delivery information. Alternatively, you can retrieve the tracking number on the order details page via this link. 
 <br />
 If your estimated delivery date has passed and you order hasn't been delivered, please Contact Us for further help.
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-4-2.png" /></p>

                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">2. Will my item be exactly the same color as what is shown on your website?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>Our color charts online have been adjusted to display color as close as possible to the color of the actual fabrics. However, camera resolution and computer monitors can mean the color may vary slightly between the photos and the actual fabric. Colors are subject to the actual dresses you get. We suggest you order a <a href="/all/swatch" target="_blank">fabric swatch</a> to view colors in person.</p>

                                        <div class="faqs-question">
                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">4. How can I make sure all of my dresses are the same color?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>Color consistency is of the utmost importance of course. However, there is a chance that there will be slight variations if dresses in same color submit several orders at different times. Because batches of fabric are produced at different times, the same fabric of the same color at different times might be slightly different. 
 <br />
 You need to order all dresses within 24 hours and contact us to tell us all the dress should be in the same color. Then, all the dresses will be cut from the same bolt of fabric to make sure they come in the exact same color.
 <br />
 After 24 hours, we cannot guarantee any late orders will be included in the same dye lot as the rest of your party.
 <br />
 Keep in mind that screen resolutions can alter the way colors look on your computer depending on how you have it set. We always recommend ordering Swatches (free shipping) beforehand so you can see the true color quality of each fabric in person. Please note that different types of fabrics do take the dye differently, and will not match perfectly.</p>
                            <div class="hide-answer-box"><a class="faqs-article-link" target="_blank" href="https://jjshouse.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360039693373-How-can-I-make-sure-all-of-my-dresses-are-the-same-color-?domain=www.jjshouse.com">Read Article<span></span></a></div>
                            <a class="faqs-article-link" target="_blank" href="https://jjshouse.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360039693373-How-can-I-make-sure-all-of-my-dresses-are-the-same-color-?domain=www.jjshouse.com">Read Article<span></span></a>

                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">4. How much does shipping cost?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>The shipping costs depend on the weight of the order, the country of destination and the shipping method, if you put all items in the cart and go to checkout, you will see the shipping costs, which are automatically calculated by the system.
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-16-1.png" />
<img style="width:100%;" data-src="https://cdn-www.jjshouse.com/public/zeus/images/live-chat/answer-16-2.png" /></p>

                                <div class="faqs-category">
                    <p class="faqs-category-title"  data-label="returns">
                        <span class="content">Returns</span>
                        <span class="fold-status open"></span>
                    </p>
                                        <div class="faqs-question">
                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">1. What is your return policy?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>JJ's House will issue a full refund including tax and shipping for any damaged, defective, or mis-shipped items. If your item arrives damaged or defective, please reach out to our Customer Service team directly for assistance with processing your return. 
 <br />
 Please keep in mind that all dresses are uniquely made to order to keep costs low for our customers. We also understand that colors on your computer screen can be a little different to how they appear in person. For these reasons, we encourage you to order a <a href="/all/swatch" target="_blank" style="font-weight: bold;">Swatch</a> (free shipping) to help you decide.
 <br />
 FOR ALL RETURNS:
 <br />
 JJ's House will only issue one prepaid return label per order. You will be responsible for paying shipping fees including, but not limited to, the cost to ship and any shipping materials on additional returns. Because of this, we recommend returning all unwanted items at one time.
 <br />
 FOR ALL STANDARD SIZE DRESSES, SHOES, AND ACCESSORIES:
 <br />
 JJ's House will issue a full refund of the cost of the returned product if you are not satisfied with your item(s). Contact our Customer Service to initiate the return process within 14 days upon receiving your item(s). The item must be returned in its original condition (if eligible per the return policy).
 <br />
 Please note:
 <br />
 * The item must be unworn, unwashed, unaltered, undamaged and with the original tags attached. We cannot process the return of any faulty item.
 <br />
 * Original shipping fee & return shipping fee will not be refunded.
 <br />
 * As all items (including standard size) are made-to-order, we cannot afford to accept the buy-many-keep-one purchase. Our customer service team may cancel an order believed to have been made with that intention.
 <br />
 FOR ALL CUSTOM SIZE DRESSES:
 <br />
 At JJ's House, we understand that you may want the dress to ideal fit! To help you out, we offer custom sizing on most of our dresses. Custom sizing takes the same amount of time to make and ship to you! 
 <br />
 A few things to remember about custom dresses:
 <br />
 Custom dresses are made specifically to the measurements you provide (bust, waist, hips, height, and hollow-to-floor). That means no one else will be able to wear that dress once it's made. Because of this, we are unable to accept any returns on custom dresses. Please double check your measurements and color choice before ordering.
 <br />
 We understand that sometimes small alterations are needed, we offer limited alterations reimbursement for only our custom sizes. Simply send us a picture of your receipt from the tailor and your order number and we'll do the rest! Yes, it really is that easy!
 <br />
 FOR ALL PRESONALIZED AND PERSONAL CARE ITEMS:
 <br />
 All personalized and personal care items (including earrings, lingerie, swimwear, etc.) are final sale. Due to hygiene issues there are no returns/exchanges.
 <br />
 FOR ALL SAMPLE SALE ITEMS:
 <br />
 All Sample Sale items are final sale. No returns, no refunds, no exchages.
 <br />
 EXCHANGE POLICY
 <br />
 We do not offer an exchange service for any products at this time. Because all items are made-to-order, we do not have ready-made dresses or products that can be shipped in exchange for your returned items. You will need to return unwanted items (if eligible per the return policy), and then place a new order for the replacement items. All new orders are subject to the current production period.
 <br />
 HOW TO RETURN
 <br />
 1. Submit a return request at Contact Us to Customer Service within 14 days of receiving your order. Please include the reason for return and photographs for verification.
 <br />
 2. Once we have approved your request, you will be sent a return form which needs to be included with your return. Please send your item(s) using local post within 14 days from receiving the return form.
 <br />
 3. When we receive the returned package, the item(s) will be inspected to ensure it is in the original condition and has the issues stated in the return request.
 <br />
 4. Once confirmed, the refund will be credited back to the original payment method within 10-15 days (the processing time depends on your payment method and bank).
 <br />
 Please note:
 <br />
 * We reserve the right to refuse the return if received in an unacceptable condition.
 <br />
 * We cannot process any products that are returned without our prior knowledge.
 <br />
 * We are not liable for return item(s) that are lost or damaged, please keep the receipt with tracking information.
 <br />
 CANCELLATION POLICY
 <br />
 All our items are made-to-order, including standard size items. Once the tailoring process has begun, there will be Labor Costs and Material Costs, with this in mind, please refer to our cancellation policy below: 
 <br />
   Unpaid orders are automatically cancelled after 5 days.
 <br />
   Cancel order within 24 hours of payment for a full refund.
 <br />
   Cancel order 2472 hours after payment: 80% refund + shipping fee.
 <br />
   Cancel order 72-120 hours after payment: 50% refund + shipping fee.
 <br />
   Cancel order > 120 hours after payment: Refund of shipping fee only.
 <br />
   Once your order is shipped, it cannot be cancelled.</p>
                            <div class="hide-answer-box"><a class="faqs-article-link" target="_blank" href="https://jjshouse.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360039199594-What-is-your-return-policy-?domain=www.jjshouse.com">Read Article<span></span></a></div>
                            <a class="faqs-article-link" target="_blank" href="https://jjshouse.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360039199594-What-is-your-return-policy-?domain=www.jjshouse.com">Read Article<span></span></a>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">

                                        <div class="faqs-question">
                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">1. Do you have a store?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>We are sorry but currently we do not have any physical stores. As an e-commerce company, we just do business online. You can see the products on our website and place the order. We will make the products for you once your order is confirmed.
 <br />
 We completely understand that you may have concerns about the fit and the style of our dresses. If so, you can choose custom size to ensure the fit. For most of adult dresses, we can make it with your measurements and the dress will fit you well. Each of our dresses is totally made to order according to our pictures. We sincerely hope you could give us a try.</p>
                            <div class="hide-answer-box"><a class="faqs-article-link" target="_blank" href="https://jjshouse.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360046608674-Do-you-have-a-store-?domain=www.jjshouse.com">Read Article<span></span></a></div>

                                        <div class="faqs-question">
                        <p class="faqs-question-title">
                            <span class="faqs-question-title-detail">2. Why choose JJ&#039;s House?</span>
                            <span class="fold-status down"></span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="faqs-answer">
                            <p>JJs House is a global online retailer. Our innovative approach brings you the best in formal wear at affordable prices  and our in-house designers have created a wide range of looks to have you dressed to impress anywhere, anytime. All our dresses are made-to-measure by our expert tailors to ensure the perfect fit, just for you.
We pride ourselves on being socially and environmentally conscious - our made-to-order model means the fabric and other materials used dont go to waste. We work in close, fair partnership with our tailors.</p>

                <div class="list-faq-container">
    
    <div class="category-title">
        Frequently Asked Questions About Wedding Dresses
    </div>
    
    <div class="expand-container">
                <details>
            <summary>
                How much does a wedding dress typically cost?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>Wedding dress prices can vary greatly depending on factors such as style, designer, and materials. At JJ's House, we understand the importance of accommodating different budgets. Our collection features a diverse range of options, including budget-friendly dresses starting at $500 and <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/collection/wedding-dresses-under-100-usd" target="_blank">stunning options priced under $100</a>. Explore our selection to find the perfect gown that suits both your style and budget.</p>
            </div>
        </details>
                <details>
            <summary>
                What is the most popular wedding dress silhouette?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>The <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/collection/a-line-wedding-dresses" target="_blank">A-line wedding dress</a> silhouette remains a beloved favorite among brides for its universally flattering shape. Featuring a fitted bodice that cinches at the waist and gently flares out to the hem, the A-line style accentuates curves while providing comfort and grace. Renowned for its timeless appeal, the A-line silhouette offers brides a classic and elegant choice for their special day.</p>
            </div>
        </details>
                <details>
            <summary>
                What type of undergarment should I wear with my wedding dress?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>The choice of <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/all/lingerie" target="_blank">undergarments for your wedding dress</a> depends on its style and design. Some dresses feature built-in support, while others may necessitate specific undergarments to achieve the desired shape and fit. For strapless dresses, a supportive bra that stays in place is often recommended. If your dress is made of thin or clingy fabric, seamless or no-show underwear can help prevent visible lines. Additionally, some brides opt for shapewear or corsets to provide extra support or create a specific silhouette. Consider the unique requirements of your dress and consult with a professional to ensure you find the perfect undergarments to enhance your wedding day look.</p>
            </div>
        </details>
                <details>
            <summary>
                When is the best time to order my wedding dress?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>To ensure a seamless wedding dress experience, it's recommended to order your dress 6-8 months before your wedding date. This timeframe allows for the creation, shipping, and necessary alterations closer to the big day. At JJ's House, we understand the urgency of rush orders. That's why we offer <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/shop/wedding-dresses" target="_blank">a range of standard size wedding dresses</a> that can be shipped within 48 hours. Take advantage of our speedy options while ensuring your dream dress arrives on time for your special celebration. Plan ahead and order your wedding dress at the perfect time for a stress-free experience.</p>
            </div>
        </details>
                <details>
            <summary>
                How do I find my wedding dress size?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>As a general guideline, starting 2-4 sizes above your pant size is recommended when selecting a bridal gown. Keep in mind that wedding dresses can usually be altered 2-4 sizes down without compromising the dress's integrity. For example, a size 14 gown can be altered to fit a size 10 while maintaining its overall design. </p>
            </div>
        </details>
                <details>
            <summary>
                Why are wedding dresses traditionally white, and can I choose a different color?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>Traditionally, white has been associated with purity and innocence, which is why white wedding dresses became popular. However, modern brides have the freedom to choose a wedding dress in any color that reflects their personal style and preferences. From soft pastels to bold hues, the options are limitless. At JJ's House, we offer a wide range of <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/all/wedding-dresses?collection=gold" target="_blank">wedding dresses in various colors</a>, allowing you to express your individuality and make a statement on your special day. Whether you opt for a traditional white gown or decide to embrace a different color, we're here to help you find the perfect dress that makes you feel confident and beautiful.</p>
            </div>
        </details>
                <details>
            <summary>
                What is your return and exchange policy for wedding dresses?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>At JJ's House, we aim to provide a seamless return experience for our customers. You have the option to choose how you'd like to return your package:<br><br>1. Return Shipping Charges:<br>You can choose to return the package by yourself at your cost. The price may vary depending on your country and the shipping company you choose. Additionally, you are responsible for confirming the return delivery status.<br>For customers from specific countries, we offer return labels for a more convenient return experience. While we do charge a return shipping fee, utilizing our return label typically results in lower costs compared to other shipping companies. With our return label, you won't need to worry about arranging return delivery.<br><br>2. Return Label Service:<br>For customers from countries with return label service, we provide return labels that you can directly attach to the front of your package. The return shipping fees will be automatically deducted from your refund amount. Please refer to our website for a list of countries eligible for return label service and their respective return shipping fee standards.<br><br>3. Without Return Label Service:<br>If you're from a country without return label service, you can still return the items by taking your package to the local post location and sending it back to us. In this case, the return shipping fee will be paid by you directly to the post location.<br><br>Exchanges<br>We do not offer an exchange service for any products at this time. Many of our items are made-to-order, so we don't keep these items in stock. If an item doesn't work out and another one is needed, a return will need to be processed for all unwanted items (if eligible per the return policy) and a new order must be placed for new items.<br><br>We strive to ensure that our return process is as convenient and transparent as possible for our valued customers. If you have any questions or require further assistance regarding returns, please don't hesitate to contact our customer service team or refer to our <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/help/returns-refund" target="_blank">returns & refunds page</a> for more information.</p>
            </div>
        </details>
                <details>
            <summary>
                Do you offer try-on services for wedding dresses?
            </summary>
            <div>
                <p>To enhance your shopping experience, we offer <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/all/try-on-wedding-dresses" target="_blank">try-on services for wedding dresses</a> in selected countries. (US, UK, DE, FR, AU, BE, AT, and CA).<br><br>Try-on services allow customers in these countries to try on their desired wedding dress before making a final decision. Please note that availability and terms may vary where you can find more information from our <a href="https://www.jjshouse.com/help/try-on-how-it-works" target="_blank">try-on services guide</a>.<br><br>We apologize for any inconvenience to customers outside of these eligible countries. However, we remain committed to providing exceptional service and are actively exploring options to expand our try-on services in the future.</p>

<script>
    if(typeof($) != 'undefined') {
        (function ($) {
            var referer = document.referrer;
            var url = document.URL;
            var re = new RegExp(/https*:\/\/(dev|ft|p|www)\.jjshouse\.com/);
            if(referer == '' || referer.search(re) == -1) {
                $.ajax({
                    type: 'POST',
                    url: webData.WEB_ROOT + 'ajax.php',
                    dataType: 'text',
                    data: {'act':'mark_referer','referer':referer,'url':url},
                    success: function(r){}
                });
            }
        })($);
    }
</script>
